var showhidden = 0;

function teamChoices(id) {
	var el = document.getElementById(id);
	teams.forEach(function(team) {
		var opt = document.createElement('option');
		opt.innerHTML = team;
		el.appendChild(opt);
	});
};

function showHide() {
	if (showhidden == 1) {
		$('.mobileout').show();
		$('#mobileout').show();
		$('.mobileonly').hide();
		$('#mobileonly').hide();
		$(".full").show();
		$("p#fullsite").html("Click Here for Mobile Site Layout");	
	} else {
		$('.mobileout').hide();
		$('#mobileout').hide();
		$('.mobileonly').show();
		$('#mobileonly').show();
		$("p#fullsite").html("Click Here or Go Landscape for Full Site Layout");
	}
	if (hasHideSelect == 1) {
		hideselect()
	}
}
if (typeof(nohighlights) == 'undefined') {

	$('html').on("click","tr",function(){

		var focusrows = $('tr:not(.highlighted)').not($('table').find('th').parent('tr').not($('.subhead, .extraheader')))
		focusrows.toggle()	
	});
	$('html').on("click","th",function(){
		$('.highlighted').removeClass('highlighted');
	})
	
})
} 
function getChicagoTimeZone() {
    // Create a Date object for the current time
    let now = new Date();

    // Get the timezone offset in minutes for Chicago (America/Chicago)
    let chicagoTime = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-US', {
        timeZone: 'America/Chicago',
        timeZoneName: 'short'
    }).formatToParts(now);

    // Find the "timeZoneName" part (it could be CST or CDT)
    let timeZoneName = chicagoTime.find(part => part.type === 'timeZoneName').value;

    return timeZoneName;  // returns "CDT" or "CST"
}
$(document).ready(function() {
	var userTimezone = Intl.DateTimeFormat().resolvedOptions().timeZone;
	$('#timeheader').attr('title', 'Your Timezone: ' + userTimezone);  
	$('.gametime').each(function() {
    // Get the time string
    var timeString = $(this).text();
	if (timeString == '') {
	    $(this).text('');
	} else {
		// Create a ate string with 'America/Chicago' timezone reference
		// Assuming today's date for the example, you might need to adjust this as per your need
		daylight = getChicagoTimeZone();
		var dateString = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US') + ' ' + timeString + ' ' + daylight;
	
		// Parse the date string in Central Time
		var centralTimeDate = new Date(dateString);
	
		// Convert to local time string without seconds
		var localTimeString = centralTimeDate.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
		  hour: '2-digit',
		  minute: '2-digit',
		  hour12: true
		});
	
		// Update the time on the page
		$(this).text(localTimeString);
	}
  });

function focusbox(t) {
	if (t == undefined || t == '') {
		 $('tr').show();	
		return
	}
 $('tr').hide();
	if (t.indexOf("~") > -1) {
		target = t.slice(1)
		if (target.indexOf("|") > -1) {
			targets = target.split("|")
			for (i = 0; i < targets.length; i++) {
				tt = targets[i];
				if (tt.indexOf("-") > -1) {
					tt = tt.slice(1)
				 	$('tr>td:contains('+tt+')').parent().hide()
				 } else {
					 $('tr>td:contains('+tt+')').parent().show()
				}
			}
		} else {
		 $('tr>td:contains('+target+')').parent().show()
		}	 

	} else if (t == 'tierA') {
		$('img[src*="/assets/a.gif"]').closest("tr").show()
	} else if (t == 'tierB') {
		$('img[src*="/assets/b.gif"]').closest("tr").show()
	} else if (t == 'tierAB') {
		$('img[src*="/assets/a.gif"]').closest("tr").show()
		$('img[src*="/assets/b.gif"]').closest("tr").show()
	} else if (t == 'HiMajor') {
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("B10")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("P10")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("P12")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("ACC")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("SEC")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("B12")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("BE")').parent().show()
	} else if (t == 'Mid') {
	$('tr>td').parent().show();
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("B10")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("P10")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("P12")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("ACC")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("SEC")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("B12")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("BE")').parent().hide()
 	$('thead:first-of-type > tr').show()
	} else if (t == 'HiAll') {
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("B10")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("P10")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("P12")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("ACC")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("SEC")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("B12")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("BE")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("Amer")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:contains("Gonzaga")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:contains("Connecticut")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:contains("Memphis")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:contains("Cincinnati")').parent().show()
	 $('tr>td:contains("Wichita St.")').parent().show()
 	$('thead:first-of-type > tr').show()
 	} else if (t == 'TruMid') {
	$('tr>td').parent().show();
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("B10")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("P10")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("P12")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("ACC")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("SEC")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("B12")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:containsExactly("BE")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:contains("Gonzaga")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:contains("Connecticut")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:contains("Memphis")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:contains("Cincinnati")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:contains("Wichita St.")').parent().hide()
	 $('tr>td:contains("Houston")').parent().hide()
	 
 	$('thead:first-of-type > tr').show()
 	} else {
		if (t.indexOf("|") > -1) {
			targets = t.split("|")
			for (i = 0; i < targets.length; i++) {
				tt = targets[i];
				 $('tr>td:containsExactly('+tt+')').parent().show()
			}
		} else {
			$('tr>td:containsExactly('+t+')').parent().show()
		 }
	}
 $('thead:first-of-type > tr').show()
	if (showhidden == 0) {
		$('.mobileout').show();
		$('#mobileout').show();
		$('.mobileonly').hide();
		$('#mobileonly').hide();
		$(".full").show();
		$("p#fullsite").html("Click Here for Mobile Site Layout");	
	} else {
		$('.mobileout').hide();
		$('#mobileout').hide();
		$('.mobileonly').show();
		$('#mobileonly').show();
		$("p#fullsite").html("Click Here or Go Landscape for Full Site Layout");
	}
 $('.mainhead').show()
}

term = ''
$('input#filterbox').attr('placeholder','Filter/Search')
$('input#filterbox').keyup(function() {
 term = $('input#filterbox').val()
 if (term != undefined) {
	focusbox(term)
}
})
$('#filterbox').keypress(function(event){
	var keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
	tterm = encodeURIComponent(term)
	if(keycode == '13' && teams.includes(term)){
		window.location.href = "https://barttorvik.com/team.php?team="+tterm;
	} else if (keycode == '13' && term.length > 5) {
		window.location.href = "https://barttorvik.com/playerstat.php?p="+tterm
	}
});


function makeCSV(source,repeat,name="trank_data.csv") {
	if (repeat == 1) {return}
	csvContent = source.join("\n")
	var link = window.document.createElement("a");
	link.setAttribute("href", "data:text/csv;charset=utf-8,%EF%BB%BF" + encodeURI(csvContent));
	link.setAttribute("download", name);
	link.click(); 
}
